Besides, AX-ZIP Extractor is simple and convenient file manager.\r\n\r\nMain Features\r\n\r\nExtraction from ZIP, CAB, RAR, JAR, XAP, GZIP, BZIP2, XZ, TAR and 7Z archives.\r\nExtraction from ISO images (ISO 9660 and ISO 13346 \"UDF\").\r\nSimultaneous work with several archives.\r\nOne drag extraction of files from archive.\r\nSearch of archives and files within the archives.\r\nBookmarks for archives and files in the archives.\r\nSupport of cloud drives and special folders.\r\nSupport of main file manager functions.\r\nSupport of drag and drop technology.\r\nDisplay of archive structure as a tree.\r\nFamiliar Explorer-like user interface.\r\n\r\nOverview\r\n\r\nAX-ZIP Extractor utility views ZIP archives and archives of other types as folders containing folders and files whose structure is shown as a tree. Thus the root folder of archive will be displayed as an icon associated with archives of that type.\r\nAX-ZIP Extractor working space is made up of two windows - Archive Browser and File Browser.\r\nArchive Browser contains a tree representing the structure of disks, folders and archives - files with extension of supported archive types. To open archive one should simply click \"+\" sign situated on the left of archive name.\r\nFile Browser shows full structure of disks, folders and files.\r\nAll operations in AX-ZIP Extractor
